Individual companies and franchises have their own underwriting criteria.\r\n\r\n$ Reasons for using payday advance loan - There are five groups that have higher odds of having used payday loans: those without a four-year college degree; home renters; African Americans; those earning below $40,000 annually; and those who are separated or divorced.\" Most borrowers use payday loans to cover ordinary living expenses over the course of months, not unexpected emergencies over the course of weeks.
